<H>{@daNDapA nrupati o subaLa girire gorekha sahita
<>bheTa hoi semAnaGku nimantraNa dei
<>nakuLara hastinA pratyagamana@}

<P>zyAmadIrgha bolikari y1eka nagra goTiy1e

<P>tahiM yAi prabeza mAdrI debIra tanay1e | 1 |

<P>se zyAmadIrgha beze zatru jita boli y1eka rAjA

<P>aruNasena nrupatira se aTai AtmajA | 2 |

<P>setubandha subaLAkaTakare se aTai Adhipati

<P>zrIrAmezwara debatAMku se khaTai anubrati | 3 |

<P>setubandhara rAjA ye aGgada kumAta

<P>tAhAra baMzare y1ehu zatru jita abatAra | 4 |

<P>aGgadara nandana ye anaGgasena nrupati

<P>indru sena bolikari ye tAhAra santati | 5 |

<P>indu senara nandana bINAy1eka boli rAjA

<P>kauzika bolikari tAhAra AtmajA | 6 |

<P>kauzikara putra ye birALa catrabratI

<P>kunda mukunda boli y1ehAra santati | 7 |

[MBO-03(2)-2]

<P>maLay1asena boLikari upujila y1ehAra bALa

<P>manumatha nrupati ye tAhAra dulALa | 8 |

<P>mamumathata nandana zatru jita nrupati

<P>belALa banare se y1ekAGga catrabratI | 9 |

<P>setubandha rAjye yAiM nakuka parabeza

<P>drumana giri pabongte uThile, bAjilA bijighoSa | 10 |

<P>ghora zabada zuNi se pachArai zatrujita nrupati

<P>kAhiMra thATha y1ere bujhani mahamantrI | 11 |

<P>rAjAra bacane mantrI hakArila pAridaNDa

<P>keuNa deza rAjAra thAThare y1e dhAmanti patacaNDa | 12 |

<P>mantrIra bacane ye bhuy1AM rAjagaNa

<P>chArilakSa yoddhA gheni dhAmanti akupAra kuLeNa | 13 |

<P>dekhile durmanaziri upare thATha achanti apramita

<P>samadaNDa gheni Asi miLile turita | 14 |

<P>re re kAra zabadare mukharAba dhunikari

<P>saini beRhile durmanagiri zatepura kari | 15 |

<P>kAhiMra re boliNa bharddhwe zabadeka hAki

<P>bAbanti siMghanAda ye hampALanti hAki | 16 |

<P>pabongtare thAiM dekhanti nakuLa saini

<P>bhaccabAca huanteNa se pAhilA ray1eNI | 17 |

<P>nakuLa boilA Are ohlAa pabongtuM

<P>basanta senApatiku boile bAratA kara tu | 18 |

<P>pANDabongkara AgyAmy1e se maLay1a basanta beni

<P>durmana giripabongtuM ohlarale kare bijekarNNakaTAra gheni | 19 |

<P1>13|2 akUpAra--samubra |

<P1>17|2 ray1eNI--rAtri |

[MBO-03(2)-3]

<P>zatru jitara saini ye bindhanti nArAja

<P>yuddha dekhi bikAzilA diguNa tAhAMkara tena | 20 |

<P>asipatra bulAiNa paDile bIre mADi

<P>paLAile kiMkara baLa pratagyAM darpa chADi | 21 |

<P>mantrIbara hakAranti raha raha mahAbaLA

<P>rahi samAsyA kara re ki nimante tumbhe paLA | 22 |

<P>sambodhanA bacane rahile gyAnabara mantrI

<P>samArjanA kari kahanti se maLay1a basanta senApati | 23 |

<P>Aho rAjAkaiM bAratA kara tumbhara yAiM

<P>bola nakuLa ThAkure y1e yujheSThi debaMka sAna bhAi | 24 |

<P>AgyAM pramANa dakSiNa digaku baraNa

<P>rAjusiyAga nimante rAjAnta nimantraNa 25 |

<P>samadaNDa gheni yibe dakSiNa digara sAta sahasra rAjA

<P>yujheSThi deba ThAkuraMku karibe yAi pAdapUjA | 26 |

<P>zuNi kopAnaLa se kiMkaragaNamAne

<P>zrIrAmahuM Ana Ambhe na jANu na zuNu karNNe | 27 |

<P>jIbanaku yebaNa rAjAra ho nicay1e nAhiM Aza

<P>zatrujitara AnaTi tumbhe rAyare na paza | 28 |

<P>Aho pratagyAM kariNa se tarjanti garjanti

<P>zALa ziLa pASANanta gheniNa bulAbanti | 29 |

<P>kSaNake sAmAnya se kSaNa kSaNake kAmarUpI

<P>kSaNake gupata huanti kSaNake gagana kSepi | 30 |

<P>antarIkSe bulAiM prahAra karanti zALa ziLa

<P>kSaNake mahabIra murati kSaNake bikaTALa | 31 |

<P>dekhiNa kopakale se nakuLara saini

<P>garjiNa uThile se bAhAtAda dhuni | 32 |

<P1>28|2 Ana--zagatha bA rANa |

[MBO-03(2)-4]

<P>kunta khaDaga ye parigha nArAja tIkSamunA

<P>chatrIMkara senApati se baDakumAra nenA | 33 |

<P>ragnabaLa paLAi yAiM kahile rAjAra chAmure | 40 |

<P>zuNimA deba sAbadhAne zatru jita daNDadhArI

<P>adabhmate saini tohora samare prANahArI | 41 |

[MBO-03(2)-5]

<P>hAtheNa kALacatreLa gheniNa nrupamaNi

[MBO-03(2)-6]

<P>muhiM toho zatu nohoi keuMNasi kALe
